<ul dir="auto">
<li>Recently, we raise a special issue on Remote Sensing (IF=5.349) from now to <del><strong>16 June 2023</strong></del> <strong>16 Dec 2023</strong>. You are welcomed to submit your manuscript at (<a href="https://www.mdpi.com/journal/remotesensing/special_issues/EMPK490239" rel="nofollow">https://www.mdpi.com/journal/remotesensing/special_issues/EMPK490239</a>), but you need to keep open-source fee in mind.</li>
</ul>
